Gro Play is a proud winner of the Swedish Living Green award 2012.\r\n\r\nThe app \"Find Adventure, Alfie Atkins\" is based on the Scandinavian children’s book classic \"Very Tricky, Alfie Atkins\" by the author Gunilla Bergström. In this app kids can continue that imaginary trip and get inspired to open up their DYI mind and to join the creating culture. We believe that kids and their parents can appreciate everyday items that surround ourselves and not to always look for the next new thing.
